name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples

rating:5
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:Yangzhou B&B brings endless surprises

During the 24h Special Forces trip in Yangzhou, I stayed at the awesome Reconstruction¬∑Ice Ou Pavilion. The food, accommodation, travel and entertainment facilities are all excellent. I don't want to check out at all!

üõåThe Ice Ou Pavilion itself was rebuilt from an old house in the Qing Dynasty, so it is named "Reconstruction¬∑Ice Ou Pavilion". Entering the Ice Ou Pavilion, you can see water, pine, bamboo, stone, calligraphy and painting, which constitute the ancient and a**ospheric sense of Chinese style. It is no exaggeration to call it a step-by-step scene. This is the first surprise. The original building was built in the form of a quadrangle. Each small courtyard also has a separate landscape, with a sense of winding paths. Checking in is like returning to your own garden in Jiangnan, and the experience is excellent. The room furnishings are exquisite and simple, showing taste, and are also equipped with professional tea sets. You can enjoy the leisure of tea tasting without going to the teahouse.
üìçThe location of the Ice Ou Pavilion is at the southeast corner of Dongguan Street, and it takes about 20 minutes to get there by taxi from the railway station. To the south of the road is Pishi Street. A few hundred meters to the west is Caiyi Street. Attractions such as Heyuan, Geyuan, and Slender West Lake can be reached on foot, which is very convenient. There are restaurants, specialty shops, lacquer fan workshops, etc. at the entrance of the hotel. If you don't go far, you can fully experience the slow life of Yangzhou by strolling at the door of your home. This is the second surprise.
üçúThe next morning, I wanted to go out to experience the morning tea culture, but I saw that the breakfast menu of the hotel's own restaurant, Bingou Pavilion¬∑Xiyan, almost included all the special dishes of Yangzhou morning tea (what I want to eat). I decided to experience the hotel's breakfast first, but I didn't expect it to be the third surprise. The breakfast of Xiyan is not the common buffet style of the hotel but a fixed menu, including green Yangchun tea, three-piece buns, thousand-layer oil cakes, hot dried silk, black vinegar sauce crystal meat, shrimp roe wontons and other dishes. It can be said that everything you should eat is included, and the taste is also excellent, especially the soup of shrimp roe wontons, which has to be filled with eyebrows after drinking. The dining environment of Xiyan is also very quiet, with exquisite landscapes in every corner, unlike the noisy teahouses outside. In this way, having breakfast at Xiyan has become a cost-effective choice to experience the Yangzhou morning tea culture.
üì±The hotel also has a dedicated butler. If you have any questions, send WeChat and the response speed is also very fast. Overall, it is a perfect hotel experience!

First of all, the service is very good. There is a butler service from the beginning of the reservation. The hotel is in a very good location, next to Dongguan Street and Pishi Street, and it is convenient to go anywhere. It is just a few steps away from the car. The environment is so good, every detail is a scene, compared to the flow of people in Geyuan and Heyuan, it is simply quiet and exquisite here, and the night view is also beautiful, and I can't stop taking pictures. Although the room I stayed in was small, the floor height was very good, the linens were comfortable, the shower water was very large and hot, and the free toiletries were super good. The most amazing thing is the breakfast. The hotel is divided into 5 major sections: accommodation, catering, cultural and creative, coffee, and tea room. In the morning, I had authentic Huaiyang morning tea, a cup of clear tea, a bowl of wonton noodles, green vegetable wraps with fresh meat buns, hot dried silk, appetizers... I came back and experienced it quietly.
